   55   static int32_T div_s32(const emlrtStack *sp, int32_T numerator, int32_T

   57   {
   58     int32_T quotient;
   59     uint32_T absNumerator;
   60     uint32_T absDenominator;
   61     boolean_T quotientNeedsNegation;
   62     if (denominator == 0) {
   63       if (numerator >= 0) {
   64         quotient = MAX_int32_T;
   65       } else {
   66         quotient = MIN_int32_T;
   67       }
   68   
   69       emlrtDivisionByZeroErrorR2012b(NULL, sp);
   70     } else {
   71       if (numerator >= 0) {
   72         absNumerator = (uint32_T)numerator;

   74         absNumerator = (uint32_T)-numerator;
   75       }
   76   
   77       if (denominator >= 0) {
   78         absDenominator = (uint32_T)denominator;
   79       } else {
   80         absDenominator = (uint32_T)-denominator;
   81       }
   82   
   83       quotientNeedsNegation = ((numerator < 0) != (denominator < 0));
   84       absNumerator /= absDenominator;
   85       if (quotientNeedsNegation) {
   86         quotient = -(int32_T)absNumerator;
   87       } else {
   88         quotient = (int32_T)absNumerator;
   89       }
   90     }
   91   
   92     return quotient;
